    /** XÃ¢y chuá»—i tráº¡ng thÃ¡i phiÃªn (dÃ¹ng chung cho nhiá»u response). */
    private String buildSessionStatusStr(AuctionSession session) {
        return "gia_hien_tai=" + session.getCurrentHighestBid()
                + "|nguoi_dan_dau=" + getWinnerUsername(session)
                + "|trang_thai=" + session.getStatus();
    }

    /** Chuyá»ƒn giÃ¡ trá»‹ null thÃ nh chuá»—i rá»—ng (trÃ¡nh "null" trong response). */
    private String nullSafe(Object obj) {
        return (obj != null) ? obj.toString() : "";
    }

    /**
     * Kiá»ƒm tra máº­t kháº©u â€” há»— trá»£ cáº£ BCrypt (má»›i) vÃ  plaintext (cÅ©, backward compat).
     * Sau khi toÃ n bá»™ user Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Äƒng kÃ½ láº¡i, cÃ³ thá»ƒ xÃ³a nhÃ¡nh plaintext.
     */
    private boolean isPasswordValid(String rawPassword, String storedPassword) {
        if (storedPassword != null && storedPassword.startsWith("$2")) {
            // BCrypt hash
            return BCrypt.verifyer()
                         .verify(rawPassword.toCharArray(), storedPassword)
                         .verified;
        }
        // Fallback plaintext (ngÆ°á»i dÃ¹ng cÅ© seed/demo)
        return rawPassword.equals(storedPassword);
    }


    /**
     * GET_MY_AUCTIONS|sellerId
     * â†’ MY_AUCTIONS|auctionId:itemName:price:status:endTime|...
     */
    private String processGetMyAuctions(String[] parts) {
        if (parts.length != 2) return "LOI|Dinh dang: GET_MY_AUCTIONS|sellerId";
        try {
            var sessions = new com.auction.server.dao.AuctionDAO().getSessionsBySeller(parts[1]);
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("MY_AUCTIONS");
            for (var s : sessions) {
                sb.append("|")
                  .append(s.getAuctionID()).append(";")
                  .append(s.getDisplayItem()).append(";")
                  .append(s.getCurrentHighestBid()).append(";")
                  .append(s.getStatus()).append(";")
                  .append(nullSafe(s.getStartTime())).append(";")
                  .append(nullSafe(s.getEndTime()));
            }
            return sb.length() == "MY_AUCTIONS".length() ? "MY_AUCTIONS|trong" : sb.toString();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi lay danh sach: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    /**
     * DELETE_AUCTION|auctionId|sellerId
     * Chá»‰ cho phÃ©p xÃ³a khi chÆ°a cÃ³ bid vÃ  seller lÃ  chá»§ phiÃªn.
     */
    private String processDeleteAuction(String[] parts, AuctionManager manager) {
        if (parts.length != 3) return "LOI|Dinh dang: DELETE_AUCTION|auctionId|sellerId";
        String auctionId = parts[1];
        String sellerId  = parts[2];
        try {
            com.auction.server.dao.AuctionDAO auctionDAO = new com.auction.server.dao.AuctionDAO();
            
            // HoÃ n láº¡i tiá»n cho bidder Ä‘ang dáº«n Ä‘áº§u (náº¿u cÃ³) trÆ°á»›c khi xÃ³a phiÃªn Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡
            com.auction.domain.AuctionSession session = manager.getSession(auctionId);
            if (session != null) {
                String leadingBidder = session.getCurrentHighestBidderID();
                double leadingAmount = session.getCurrentHighestBid();
                if (leadingBidder != null && !leadingBidder.isBlank()) {
                    try {
                        com.auction.server.dao.UserDAO userDAO = new com.auction.server.dao.UserDAO();
                        com.auction.common.models.User user = userDAO.findById(leadingBidder);
                        if (user instanceof com.auction.common.models.Bidder bidder) {
                            bidder.getWallet().release(leadingAmount);
                            userDAO.saveUser(bidder);
                            System.out.printf("[SERVER] Hoan lai %.0f cho bidder %s khi seller xoa phien %s%n",
                                leadingAmount, leadingBidder, auctionId);
                        }
                    } catch (Exception e) {
                        System.err.println("[SERVER] Loi hoan tien cho bidder khi xoa phien: " + e.getMessage());
                    }
                }
            }

            // XÃ³a khá»i AuctionManager (in-memory)
            manager.removeSession(auctionId);
            // XÃ³a khá»i DB (báº£ng auction_sessions)
            auctionDAO.deleteSession(auctionId);
            // XÃ³a cÃ¡c bid liÃªn quan trong DB
            try {
                auctionDAO.deleteBidsByAuction(auctionId);
            } catch (Exception e) {
                System.err.println("[SERVER] Loi xoa bid transactions: " + e.getMessage());
            }
            return "DELETE_AUCTION_SUCCESS|" + auctionId;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi xoa phien: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    /**
     * UPDATE_AUCTION|auctionId|sellerId|newItemName
     * Chá»‰ cho phÃ©p sá»­a khi chÆ°a cÃ³ bid vÃ  seller lÃ  chá»§ phiÃªn.
     */
    private String processUpdateAuction(String[] parts, AuctionManager manager) {
        if (parts.length != 4) return "LOI|Dinh dang: UPDATE_AUCTION|auctionId|sellerId|newItemName";
        String auctionId   = parts[1];
        String newItemName = parts[3];
        try {
            com.auction.server.dao.AuctionDAO auctionDAO = new com.auction.server.dao.AuctionDAO();
            
            // Láº¥y session Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm tra tráº¡ng thÃ¡i vÃ  tÃ¬m itemId
            com.auction.domain.AuctionSession session = manager.getSession(auctionId);
            if (session == null) return "LOI|Khong tim thay phien: " + auctionId;

            // Chá»‰ cho phÃ©p sá»­a khi phiÃªn Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡ chÆ°a báº¯t Ä‘áº§u (status == PENDING)
            if (session.getStatus() != com.auction.domain.AuctionStatus.PENDING) {
                return "LOI|Khong the sua: phien dau gia da hoac dang bat dau (trang thai hien tai: " + session.getStatus() + ")";
            }

            // Cáº­p nháº­t tÃªn item trong DB
            auctionDAO.updateItemName(session.getItemID(), newItemName);
            // Cáº­p nháº­t tÃªn hiá»ƒn thá»‹ in-memory
            session.setDisplayItem(newItemName);
            return "UPDATE_AUCTION_SUCCESS|" + auctionId;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi cap nhat phien: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    /**
     * CLOSE_SESSION|auctionId â€” Admin Ä‘Ã³ng phiÃªn thá»§ cÃ´ng.
     */
    private String processCloseSession(String[] parts, AuctionManager manager) {
        if (parts.length != 2) return "LOI|Dinh dang: CLOSE_SESSION|auctionId";
        boolean ok = manager.closeSession(parts[1]);
        if (!ok) return "LOI|Khong the dong phien (khong ton tai hoac da dong): " + parts[1];

        // Broadcast káº¿t thÃºc tá»›i táº¥t cáº£ client
        server.broadcast("CAP_NHAT|id=" + parts[1]
                + "|trang_thai=FINISHED|gia_hien_tai=0|nguoi_dan_dau=");
        logActivity("ADMIN", "CLOSE_SESSION", "Phien: " + parts[1]);
        return "CLOSE_SESSION_SUCCESS|" + parts[1];
    }

    /**
     * DEPOSIT|bidderId|amount â€” Náº¡p tiá»n vÃ o vÃ­ Bidder.
     */
    private String processDeposit(String[] parts) {
        if (parts.length != 3) return "LOI|Dinh dang: DEPOSIT|bidderId|amount";
        double amount;
        try {
            amount = Double.parseDouble(parts[2]);
        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
            return "LOI|So tien phai la so";
        }
        if (amount <= 0) return "LOI|So tien phai lon hon 0";
        try {
            UserDAO userDAO = new UserDAO();
            User user = userDAO.findById(parts[1]);
            if (!(user instanceof Bidder bidder)) return "LOI|Khong tim thay Bidder: " + parts[1];
            bidder.getWallet().deposit(amount);
            userDAO.saveUser(bidder);
            logActivity(parts[1], "DEPOSIT", "So tien: " + amount);
            return "DEPOSIT_SUCCESS|" + bidder.getWallet().getBalance();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi nap tien: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    private String getWinnerUsername(AuctionSession session) {
        String winnerId = session.getWinnerID();
        if (winnerId == null || winnerId.isBlank()) {
            return "";
        }
        try {
            User user = new UserDAO().findById(winnerId);
            if (user != null) {
                return user.getUsername();
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.err.println("[SERVER] Lá»—i tÃ¬m username cho winnerID " + winnerId + ": " + e.getMessage());
        }
        return winnerId;
    }

    /** Giáº£i phÃ³ng tÃ i nguyÃªn khi client ngáº¯t káº¿t ná»‘i. */
    private void cleanup() {
        server.unregisterUser(loggedInUserId);
        server.removeClient(this);
        try {
            if (!socket.isClosed()) socket.close();
        } catch (IOException ignored) { }
    }

    private String processGetProfile(String[] parts) {

                    + bidder.getWallet().getBalance() + "|"

        }
    }
    /**
     * GET_MY_BIDS|bidderId
     * â†’ MY_BIDS|auctionId;itemName;bidAmount;status|...
     */
    private String processGetMyBids(String[] parts) {
        if (parts.length != 2) return "LOI|Dinh dang: GET_MY_BIDS|bidderId";
        try {
            // Láº¥y táº¥t cáº£ bid cá»§a bidder nÃ y
            String sql = """
                SELECT bt.auction_id, COALESCE(i.name, bt.auction_id) as item_name,
                    bt.bid_amount, s.status
                FROM bid_transactions bt
                LEFT JOIN auction_sessions s ON bt.auction_id = s.auction_id
                LEFT JOIN items i ON s.item_id = i.id
                WHERE bt.bidder_id = ?
                ORDER BY bt.bid_time DESC
                """;

            java.util.Map<String, String[]> latest = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
            try (var conn = com.auction.server.util.DatabaseUtil.getInstance().getConnection();
                var stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
                stmt.setString(1, parts[1]);
                var rs = stmt.executeQuery();
                while (rs.next()) {
                    String aid = rs.getString("auction_id");
                    // Chá»‰ giá»¯ bid má»›i nháº¥t má»—i phiÃªn
                    if (!latest.containsKey(aid)) {
                        latest.put(aid, new String[]{
                            aid,
                            rs.getString("item_name"),
                            String.valueOf(rs.getDouble("bid_amount")),
                            rs.getString("status")
                        });
                    }
                }
            }

            if (latest.isEmpty()) return "MY_BIDS|trong";

            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("MY_BIDS");
            for (var entry : latest.values()) {
                sb.append("|")
                .append(entry[0]).append(";")
                .append(entry[1]).append(";")
                .append(entry[2]).append(";")
                .append(entry[3]);
            }
            return sb.toString();

        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi lay my bids: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    private String processGetNotifications(String[] parts) {
        if (parts.length != 2) return "LOI|Dinh dang: GET_NOTIFICATIONS|userId";
        try {
            var list = new NotificationDAO().getByUser(parts[1]);
            if (list.isEmpty()) return "NOTIFICATIONS|trong";
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("NOTIFICATIONS");
            for (String[] n : list) {
                // id;type;content;auctionId;isRead;createdAt
                sb.append("|")
                .append(n[0]).append(";")
                .append(n[1]).append(";")
                .append(n[2]).append(";")
                .append(n[3]).append(";")
                .append(n[4]).append(";")
                .append(n[5]);
            }
            return sb.toString();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|" + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    private String processMarkNotificationsRead(String[] parts) {
        if (parts.length != 2) return "LOI|Dinh dang: MARK_NOTIFICATIONS_READ|userId";
        try {
            new NotificationDAO().markAllRead(parts[1]);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|" + e.getMessage();
        }
        return "MARK_READ_SUCCESS";
    }

        /**
     * BAN_USER|targetUsername|ban (true/false)
     */
    private String processBanUser(String[] parts) {
        if (parts.length != 3) return "LOI|Dinh dang: BAN_USER|username|true/false";
        try {
            UserDAO userDAO = new UserDAO();
            User target = userDAO.getUserByUsername(parts[1]);
            if (target == null) return "LOI|Khong tim thay user: " + parts[1];
            boolean ban = Boolean.parseBoolean(parts[2]);
            try (var conn = com.auction.server.util.DatabaseUtil.getInstance().getConnection();
                var stmt = conn.prepareStatement(
                        "UPDATE users SET is_banned = ? WHERE username = ?")) {
                stmt.setInt(1, ban ? 1 : 0);
                stmt.setString(2, parts[1]);
                stmt.executeUpdate();
            }
            // Ghi log
            logActivity("ADMIN", ban ? "BAN_USER" : "UNBAN_USER", "Target: " + parts[1]);
            return ban ? "BAN_SUCCESS|" + parts[1] : "UNBAN_SUCCESS|" + parts[1];
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|" + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    /**
     * GET_ACTIVITY_LOG â€” láº¥y 100 log gáº§n nháº¥t
     */
    private String processGetActivityLog(String[] parts) {
        try {
            String sql = """
                    SELECT user_id, action, detail, created_at
                    FROM activity_log
                    ORDER BY created_at DESC
                    LIMIT 100
                    """;
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("ACTIVITY_LOG");
            try (var conn = com.auction.server.util.DatabaseUtil.getInstance().getConnection();
                var stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
                var rs   = stmt.executeQuery()) {
                while (rs.next()) {
                    sb.append("|")
                    .append(rs.getString("user_id")).append(";")
                    .append(rs.getString("action")).append(";")
                    .append(rs.getString("detail") != null ? rs.getString("detail") : "").append(";")
                    .append(rs.getString("created_at"));
                }
            }
            return sb.length() == "ACTIVITY_LOG".length()
                    ? "ACTIVITY_LOG|trong" : sb.toString();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|" + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    private void logActivity(String userId, String action, String detail) {
        try {
            String sql = "INSERT INTO activity_log (user_id, action, detail, created_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
            try (var conn = com.auction.server.util.DatabaseUtil.getInstance().getConnection();
                var stmt = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
                stmt.setString(1, userId);
                stmt.setString(2, action);
                stmt.setString(3, detail);
                stmt.setString(4, java.time.LocalDateTime.now()
                        .format(java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss")));
                stmt.executeUpdate();
            }
        } catch (Exception ignored) {}
    }

package com.auction.server.service;

import com.auction.server.dao.NotificationDAO;
import com.auction.server.dao.UserDAO;
import com.auction.server.network.AuctionServer;
import com.auction.common.models.User;

import java.util.List;

/**
 * Service táº­p trung toÃ n bá»™ logic táº¡o vÃ  gá»­i notification.
 *
 * <p>Luá»“ng hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng:
 * <ol>
 *   <li>Ghi vÃ o DB (NotificationDAO.save) Ä‘á»ƒ lÆ°u lá»‹ch sá»­.</li>
 *   <li>Push realtime qua socket náº¿u user Ä‘ang online
 *       ({@link AuctionServer#sendToUser}).</li>
 * </ol>
 * </p>
 *
 * <p>Format tin nháº¯n socket:
 * {@code NOTIFICATION|type|content|auctionId}
 * </p>
 *
 * <p>ÄÆ°á»£c gá»i tá»« {@link com.auction.server.network.ClientHandler} sau má»—i sá»± kiá»‡n
 * quan trá»ng (bid má»›i, káº¿t thÃºc phiÃªn, anti-snipe, v.v.).</p>
 */
public class NotificationService {

    // Loáº¡i notification â€” dÃ¹ng lÃ m háº±ng sá»‘ Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh typo
    public static final String TYPE_BID_OUTBID      = "BID_OUTBID";       // Bidder bá»‹ vÆ°á»£t máº·t
    public static final String TYPE_AUCTION_WON     = "AUCTION_WON";      // Bidder tháº¯ng cuá»™c
    public static final String TYPE_AUCTION_LOST    = "AUCTION_LOST";     // Bidder thua cuá»™c
    public static final String TYPE_AUCTION_ENDING  = "AUCTION_ENDING";   // PhiÃªn sáº¯p káº¿t thÃºc (5 phÃºt)
    public static final String TYPE_ANTI_SNIPE      = "ANTI_SNIPE";       // PhiÃªn bá»‹ gia háº¡n
    public static final String TYPE_BID_PLACED      = "BID_PLACED";       // Seller: cÃ³ ngÆ°á»i Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡
    public static final String TYPE_SESSION_CREATED = "SESSION_CREATED";  // Seller: táº¡o phiÃªn thÃ nh cÃ´ng
    public static final String TYPE_SESSION_ENDED   = "SESSION_ENDED";    // Seller: phiÃªn káº¿t thÃºc

    private final NotificationDAO notificationDAO;
    private final AuctionServer   server;

    public NotificationService(AuctionServer server) {
        this.notificationDAO = new NotificationDAO();
        this.server          = server;
    }

    // =========================================================================
    // API cÃ´ng khai â€” gá»i tá»« ClientHandler / Scheduler
    // =========================================================================

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // BIDDER notifications
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    /**
     * Bidder bá»‹ vÆ°á»£t máº·t bá»Ÿi ngÆ°á»i khÃ¡c.
     *
     * @param outbidBidderId ID bidder bá»‹ vÆ°á»£t
     * @param auctionId      ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName       TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     * @param newPrice       GiÃ¡ má»›i (cá»§a ngÆ°á»i vá»«a vÆ°á»£t)
     */
    public void notifyBidderOutbid(String outbidBidderId,
                                   String auctionId,
                                   String itemName,
                                   double newPrice) {
        String content = String.format(
                "Báº¡n vá»«a bá»‹ vÆ°á»£t máº·t táº¡i phiÃªn \"%s\"! GiÃ¡ má»›i: %,.0f â‚«. Äáº·t giÃ¡ ngay Ä‘á»ƒ giÃ nh láº¡i!",
                itemName, newPrice);
        send(outbidBidderId, TYPE_BID_OUTBID, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * Bidder tháº¯ng cuá»™c khi phiÃªn káº¿t thÃºc.
     *
     * @param winnerId   ID bidder tháº¯ng
     * @param auctionId  ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName   TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     * @param finalPrice GiÃ¡ tháº¯ng cuá»™c
     */
    public void notifyBidderWon(String winnerId,
                                String auctionId,
                                String itemName,
                                double finalPrice) {
        String content = String.format(
                "ðŸŽ‰ ChÃºc má»«ng! Báº¡n Ä‘Ã£ tháº¯ng phiÃªn \"%s\" vá»›i giÃ¡ %,.0f â‚«!",
                itemName, finalPrice);
        send(winnerId, TYPE_AUCTION_WON, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * Bidder thua cuá»™c khi phiÃªn káº¿t thÃºc (Ä‘Ã£ tá»«ng Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡ nhÆ°ng khÃ´ng tháº¯ng).
     *
     * @param loserId    ID bidder thua
     * @param auctionId  ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName   TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     * @param finalPrice GiÃ¡ tháº¯ng cuá»™c (cá»§a ngÆ°á»i khÃ¡c)
     */
    public void notifyBidderLost(String loserId,
                                  String auctionId,
                                  String itemName,
                                  double finalPrice) {
        String content = String.format(
                "PhiÃªn \"%s\" Ä‘Ã£ káº¿t thÃºc. Ráº¥t tiáº¿c, báº¡n khÃ´ng tháº¯ng. GiÃ¡ cuá»‘i: %,.0f â‚«.",
                itemName, finalPrice);
        send(loserId, TYPE_AUCTION_LOST, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * Cáº£nh bÃ¡o phiÃªn sáº¯p káº¿t thÃºc (cÃ²n 5 phÃºt) â€” gá»­i cho táº¥t cáº£ bidder Ä‘ang tham gia.
     *
     * @param bidderId  ID bidder
     * @param auctionId ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName  TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     */
    public void notifyAuctionEnding(String bidderId,
                                     String auctionId,
                                     String itemName) {
        String content = String.format(
                "â° PhiÃªn \"%s\" cÃ²n dÆ°á»›i 5 phÃºt! Äá»«ng bá» lá»¡ cÆ¡ há»™i.",
                itemName);
        send(bidderId, TYPE_AUCTION_ENDING, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * PhiÃªn bá»‹ gia háº¡n do anti-sniping â€” gá»­i cho bidder Ä‘ang xem phiÃªn.
     *
     * @param bidderId   ID bidder
     * @param auctionId  ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName   TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     * @param newEndTime Thá»i gian káº¿t thÃºc má»›i (ISO string)
     */
    public void notifyAntiSnipe(String bidderId,
                                 String auctionId,
                                 String itemName,
                                 String newEndTime) {
        String content = String.format(
                "ðŸ”” PhiÃªn \"%s\" Ä‘Æ°á»£c gia háº¡n do cÃ³ bid má»›i vÃ o phÃºt cuá»‘i! Káº¿t thÃºc lÃºc: %s.",
                itemName, newEndTime);
        send(bidderId, TYPE_ANTI_SNIPE, content, auctionId);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // SELLER notifications
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    /**
     * Seller vá»«a táº¡o phiÃªn thÃ nh cÃ´ng.
     *
     * @param sellerId  ID seller
     * @param auctionId ID phiÃªn vá»«a táº¡o
     * @param itemName  TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     */
    public void notifySellerSessionCreated(String sellerId,
                                            String auctionId,
                                            String itemName) {
        String content = String.format(
                "âœ… PhiÃªn Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡ \"%s\" (ID: %s) Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c táº¡o thÃ nh cÃ´ng!",
                itemName, auctionId);
        send(sellerId, TYPE_SESSION_CREATED, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * CÃ³ ngÆ°á»i Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡ má»›i vÃ o phiÃªn cá»§a Seller.
     *
     * @param sellerId    ID seller
     * @param auctionId   ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName    TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     * @param bidderName  Username cá»§a bidder
     * @param newPrice    GiÃ¡ vá»«a Ä‘áº·t
     */
    public void notifySellerNewBid(String sellerId,
                                    String auctionId,
                                    String itemName,
                                    String bidderName,
                                    double newPrice) {
        String content = String.format(
                "ðŸ’° \"%s\" vá»«a Ä‘áº·t %,.0f â‚« cho phiÃªn \"%s\".",
                bidderName, newPrice, itemName);
        send(sellerId, TYPE_BID_PLACED, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * PhiÃªn sáº¯p káº¿t thÃºc (cÃ²n 5 phÃºt) â€” gá»­i cho Seller.
     *
     * @param sellerId  ID seller
     * @param auctionId ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName  TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     */
    public void notifySellerAuctionEnding(String sellerId,
                                           String auctionId,
                                           String itemName) {
        String content = String.format(
                "â° PhiÃªn \"%s\" cá»§a báº¡n cÃ²n dÆ°á»›i 5 phÃºt!",
                itemName);
        send(sellerId, TYPE_AUCTION_ENDING, content, auctionId);
    }

    /**
     * PhiÃªn cá»§a Seller vá»«a káº¿t thÃºc.
     *
     * @param sellerId   ID seller
     * @param auctionId  ID phiÃªn
     * @param itemName   TÃªn sáº£n pháº©m
     * @param winnerName Username ngÆ°á»i tháº¯ng (hoáº·c null náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ ai Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡)
     * @param finalPrice GiÃ¡ cuá»‘i
     */
    public void notifySellerSessionEnded(String sellerId,
                                          String auctionId,
                                          String itemName,
                                          String winnerName,
                                          double finalPrice) {
        String content;
        if (winnerName == null || winnerName.isBlank()) {
            content = String.format(
                    "PhiÃªn \"%s\" Ä‘Ã£ káº¿t thÃºc. KhÃ´ng cÃ³ ai Ä‘áº·t giÃ¡.", itemName);
        } else {
            content = String.format(
                    "ðŸ PhiÃªn \"%s\" Ä‘Ã£ káº¿t thÃºc. NgÆ°á»i tháº¯ng: %s vá»›i giÃ¡ %,.0f â‚«.",
                    itemName, winnerName, finalPrice);
        }
        send(sellerId, TYPE_SESSION_ENDED, content, auctionId);
    }

    // =========================================================================
    // Láº¥y notification cho client (REST-style request)
    // =========================================================================

    /**
     * Láº¥y danh sÃ¡ch notification cá»§a user dáº¡ng pipe-string.
     * Format: {@code NOTIFICATIONS|id;type;content;auctionId;isRead;createdAt|...}
     */
    public String buildGetResponse(String userId) {
        try {
            List<String[]> list = notificationDAO.getByUser(userId);
            if (list.isEmpty()) return "NOTIFICATIONS|trong";
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("NOTIFICATIONS");
            for (String[] row : list) {
                // row: [id, type, content, auctionId, isRead, createdAt]
                sb.append("|")
                  .append(row[0]).append(";")
                  .append(row[1]).append(";")
                  .append(row[2].replace("|", "ï½œ").replace(";", "ï¼›")).append(";")
                  .append(row[3]).append(";")
                  .append(row[4]).append(";")
                  .append(row[5]);
            }
            return sb.toString();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi lay notifications: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    /**
     * ÄÃ¡nh dáº¥u táº¥t cáº£ notification cá»§a user lÃ  Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘á»c.
     * Tráº£ vá» "MARK_READ_SUCCESS" hoáº·c "LOI|..."
     */
    public String markAllRead(String userId) {
        try {
            notificationDAO.markAllRead(userId);
            return "MARK_READ_SUCCESS";
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return "LOI|Loi danh dau da doc: " + e.getMessage();
        }
    }

    // =========================================================================
    // Private helper
    // =========================================================================

    /**
     * Ghi DB + push socket realtime.
     */
    private void send(String userId, String type, String content, String auctionId) {
        // 1. Ghi vÃ o DB
        try {
            notificationDAO.save(userId, type, content, auctionId);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.err.println("[NOTI] Lá»—i lÆ°u DB: " + e.getMessage());
        }

        // 2. Push realtime qua socket náº¿u user Ä‘ang online
        // Format: NOTIFICATION|type|content|auctionId
        String socketMsg = "NOTIFICATION|" + type + "|"
                + content.replace("|", "ï½œ") + "|"
                + (auctionId != null ? auctionId : "");
        server.sendToUser(userId, socketMsg);
    }
}

package com.auction.server.util;

import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariConfig;
import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariDataSource;

import java.io.InputStream;
import java.sql.Connection;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.Properties;

/**
 * Singleton cung cáº¥p Connection Pool (HikariCP) cho toÃ n bá»™ server.
 *
 * <p>Thay tháº¿ design cÅ© (má»™t Connection duy nháº¥t) vá»‘n khÃ´ng thread-safe
 * khi nhiá»u ClientHandler cháº¡y song song.</p>
 *
 * <p>Má»—i láº§n gá»i {@link #getConnection()} tráº£ vá» má»™t Connection riÃªng tá»« pool.
 * Caller PHáº¢I Ä‘Ã³ng Connection báº±ng try-with-resources hoáº·c {@code conn.close()}
 * Ä‘á»ƒ tráº£ Connection vá» pool.</p>
 */
public final class DatabaseUtil {

    private static volatile DatabaseUtil instance;
    private final HikariDataSource dataSource;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Khá»Ÿi táº¡o (private constructor â€” Singleton Pattern)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    private DatabaseUtil() {
        Properties props = loadProperties();

        HikariConfig config = new HikariConfig();
        config.setJdbcUrl(props.getProperty("db.url",
                "jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/auction_system?allowPublicKeyRetrieval=true&useSSL=false&serverTimezone=UTC"));
        config.setUsername(props.getProperty("db.username", "root"));
        config.setPassword(props.getProperty("db.password", ""));

        // KÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c pool: tá»‘i Ä‘a 20, giá»¯ sáºµn 5 connection nhÃ n rá»—i
        config.setMaximumPoolSize(20);
        config.setMinimumIdle(5);

        // Timeout Ä‘á»£i láº¥y connection tá»« pool (30 giÃ¢y)
        config.setConnectionTimeout(30_000);
        // ÄÃ³ng connection nhÃ n rá»—i sau 10 phÃºt
        config.setIdleTimeout(600_000);
        // VÃ²ng Ä‘á»i tá»‘i Ä‘a cá»§a má»—i connection (30 phÃºt) â€” trÃ¡nh stale connection
        config.setMaxLifetime(1_800_000);
        // CÃ¢u SQL kiá»ƒm tra connection cÃ²n sá»‘ng khÃ´ng
        config.setConnectionTestQuery("SELECT 1");

        config.setPoolName("AuctionPool");

        this.dataSource = new HikariDataSource(config);
        System.out.println("[DATABASE] âœ“ Connection Pool khá»Ÿi táº¡o thÃ nh cÃ´ng (max=" + config.getMaximumPoolSize() + ")");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Double-Checked Locking Singleton
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    public static DatabaseUtil getInstance() {
        if (instance == null) {
            synchronized (DatabaseUtil.class) {
                if (instance == null) {
                    instance = new DatabaseUtil();
                }
            }
        }
        return instance;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Public API
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    /**
     * Láº¥y má»™t Connection tá»« pool.
     * <strong>Pháº£i Ä‘Ã³ng Connection sau khi dÃ¹ng xong</strong> (dÃ¹ng try-with-resources).
     */
    public Connection getConnection() throws SQLException {
        if (isJUnitTest()) {
            throw new SQLException("Database disabled in JUnit test mode to prevent data pollution.");
        }
        return dataSource.getConnection();
    }

    private static boolean isJUnitTest() {
        for (StackTraceElement element : Thread.currentThread().getStackTrace()) {
            if (element.getClassName().startsWith("org.junit.")) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    /** ÄÃ³ng toÃ n bá»™ pool â€” gá»i khi server táº¯t. */
    public void shutdown() {
        if (!dataSource.isClosed()) {
            dataSource.close();
            System.out.println("[DATABASE] Pool Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Ã³ng.");
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Helpers
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    private Properties loadProperties() {
        Properties props = new Properties();
        try (InputStream in = getClass().getClassLoader()
                .getResourceAsStream("config/application.properties")) {
            if (in != null) {
                props.load(in);
            } else {
                System.err.println("[DATABASE] âš  KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y application.properties, dÃ¹ng giÃ¡ trá»‹ máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh.");
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            System.err.println("[DATABASE] âš  Lá»—i Ä‘á»c properties: " + e.getMessage());
        }
        return props;
    }
}

package com.auction.server.util;

import javafx.event.ActionEvent;
import javafx.fxml.FXMLLoader;
import javafx.scene.Node;
import javafx.scene.Parent;
import javafx.scene.Scene;
import javafx.stage.Stage;

import java.io.IOException;

public class SceneUtil {
    public static void changeScene(ActionEvent event, String fxmlFile, String title) {
        try {
            Parent root = FXMLLoader.load(SceneUtil.class.getResource("/fxml/" + fxmlFile));
            Stage stage = (Stage) ((Node) event.getSource()).getScene().getWindow();
            stage.setTitle(title);
            stage.setScene(new Scene(root));
            stage.show();
        } catch (IOException e) {
            System.err.println("Khong tim thay file " + fxmlFile);
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
}

package com.auction.common.models;

import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;

/**
 * Unit test toÃ n diá»‡n cho {@link Wallet}.
 *
 * <p>Kiá»ƒm tra cÃ¡c trÆ°á»ng há»£p biÃªn (edge cases): sá»‘ Ã¢m, zero, vÆ°á»£t sá»‘ dÆ°,
 * chuá»—i thao tÃ¡c phá»©c táº¡p, vÃ  tÃ­nh nháº¥t quÃ¡n cá»§a balance + frozenAmount.</p>
 */
@DisplayName("Wallet â€” Unit Tests")
class WalletTest {

    private Wallet wallet;

    @BeforeEach
    void setUp() {
        wallet = new Wallet();
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i ban Ä‘áº§u
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Khá»Ÿi táº¡o: balance vÃ  frozenAmount Ä‘á»u báº±ng 0")
    void initialState_shouldBeZero() {
        assertEquals(0.0, wallet.getBalance(),      "Balance ban Ä‘áº§u = 0");
        assertEquals(0.0, wallet.getFrozenAmount(), "FrozenAmount ban Ä‘áº§u = 0");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Deposit
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Deposit sá»‘ dÆ°Æ¡ng: tÄƒng balance")
    void deposit_positiveAmount_shouldIncreaseBalance() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        assertEquals(1_000_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Deposit sá»‘ Ã¢m: khÃ´ng thay Ä‘á»•i balance")
    void deposit_negativeAmount_shouldBeIgnored() {
        wallet.deposit(-500.0);
        assertEquals(0.0, wallet.getBalance(), "Deposit Ã¢m bá»‹ bá» qua");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Deposit zero: khÃ´ng thay Ä‘á»•i balance")
    void deposit_zero_shouldBeIgnored() {
        wallet.deposit(0.0);
        assertEquals(0.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Nhiá»u láº§n deposit: cá»™ng dá»“n Ä‘Ãºng")
    void deposit_multipleTimes_shouldAccumulate() {
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);
        wallet.deposit(300_000.0);
        wallet.deposit(200_000.0);
        assertEquals(1_000_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Withdraw
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Withdraw há»£p lá»‡: trá»« balance, tráº£ true")
    void withdraw_validAmount_shouldDecreaseBalanceAndReturnTrue() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        assertTrue(wallet.withdraw(400_000.0));
        assertEquals(600_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Withdraw vÆ°á»£t sá»‘ dÆ°: bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i, balance khÃ´ng Ä‘á»•i")
    void withdraw_exceedingBalance_shouldReturnFalseAndLeaveBalanceUnchanged() {
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);
        assertFalse(wallet.withdraw(700_000.0));
        assertEquals(500_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Withdraw sá»‘ Ã¢m: bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i")
    void withdraw_negativeAmount_shouldReturnFalse() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        assertFalse(wallet.withdraw(-100.0));
        assertEquals(1_000_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Withdraw zero: bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i")
    void withdraw_zero_shouldReturnFalse() {
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);
        assertFalse(wallet.withdraw(0.0));
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Withdraw chÃ­nh xÃ¡c báº±ng balance: thÃ nh cÃ´ng, balance = 0")
    void withdraw_exactBalance_shouldSucceed() {
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);
        assertTrue(wallet.withdraw(500_000.0));
        assertEquals(0.0, wallet.getBalance());
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Freeze
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Freeze há»£p lá»‡: chuyá»ƒn tiá»n tá»« balance sang frozenAmount")
    void freeze_validAmount_shouldTransferFromBalanceToFrozen() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        assertTrue(wallet.freeze(300_000.0));
        assertEquals(700_000.0, wallet.getBalance(),      "Balance giáº£m");
        assertEquals(300_000.0, wallet.getFrozenAmount(), "FrozenAmount tÄƒng");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Freeze vÆ°á»£t sá»‘ dÆ°: bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i, khÃ´ng thay Ä‘á»•i state")
    void freeze_exceedingBalance_shouldReturnFalseAndLeaveStateUnchanged() {
        wallet.deposit(200_000.0);
        assertFalse(wallet.freeze(500_000.0));
        assertEquals(200_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
        assertEquals(0.0,       wallet.getFrozenAmount());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Freeze sá»‘ Ã¢m: bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i")
    void freeze_negativeAmount_shouldReturnFalse() {
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);
        assertFalse(wallet.freeze(-100.0));
        assertEquals(500_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
        assertEquals(0.0,       wallet.getFrozenAmount());
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Release
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Release há»£p lá»‡: chuyá»ƒn tiá»n tá»« frozenAmount vá» balance")
    void release_validAmount_shouldTransferFromFrozenToBalance() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        wallet.freeze(400_000.0);

        wallet.release(400_000.0);

        assertEquals(1_000_000.0, wallet.getBalance(),      "Balance Ä‘Æ°á»£c phá»¥c há»“i Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§");
        assertEquals(0.0,         wallet.getFrozenAmount(), "FrozenAmount vá» 0");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Release má»™t pháº§n frozenAmount: chá»‰ hoÃ n má»™t pháº§n")
    void release_partialAmount_shouldOnlyReleaseSpecifiedAmount() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        wallet.freeze(600_000.0);

        wallet.release(200_000.0);

        assertEquals(600_000.0, wallet.getBalance(),       "Balance tÄƒng Ä‘Ãºng pháº§n Ä‘Æ°á»£c release");
        assertEquals(400_000.0, wallet.getFrozenAmount(),  "FrozenAmount giáº£m Ä‘Ãºng");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Release vÆ°á»£t frozenAmount: bá»‹ bá» qua")
    void release_exceedingFrozenAmount_shouldBeIgnored() {
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);
        wallet.freeze(100_000.0);

        wallet.release(999_000.0); // Nhiá»u hÆ¡n frozen

        // State khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c thay Ä‘á»•i
        assertEquals(400_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
        assertEquals(100_000.0, wallet.getFrozenAmount());
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Ká»‹ch báº£n tá»•ng há»£p (phá»ng theo luá»“ng Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡ thá»±c táº¿)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Ká»‹ch báº£n Ä‘áº¥u giÃ¡: deposit â†’ freeze â†’ bá»‹ vÆ°á»£t máº·t â†’ release â†’ bid láº¡i")
    void scenario_bidThenRefundThenBidAgain_shouldMaintainConsistency() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);

        // Bid láº§n 1: freeze 300k
        assertTrue(wallet.freeze(300_000.0));
        assertEquals(700_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
        assertEquals(300_000.0, wallet.getFrozenAmount());

        // Bá»‹ vÆ°á»£t máº·t: release 300k
        wallet.release(300_000.0);
        assertEquals(1_000_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
        assertEquals(0.0,         wallet.getFrozenAmount());

        // Bid láº§n 2 vá»›i giÃ¡ cao hÆ¡n: freeze 800k
        assertTrue(wallet.freeze(800_000.0));
        assertEquals(200_000.0, wallet.getBalance());
        assertEquals(800_000.0, wallet.getFrozenAmount());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Chuá»—i thao tÃ¡c phá»©c táº¡p: tá»•ng balance + frozen pháº£i khÃ´ng Ä‘á»•i")
    void invariant_totalBalancePlusFrozenShouldEqualTotalDeposited() {
        wallet.deposit(1_000_000.0);
        wallet.freeze(300_000.0);
        wallet.withdraw(100_000.0);   // RÃºt tá»« balance cÃ²n láº¡i
        wallet.release(100_000.0);    // HoÃ n má»™t pháº§n frozen
        wallet.deposit(500_000.0);    // Náº¡p thÃªm

        double total = wallet.getBalance() + wallet.getFrozenAmount();
        // Deposit tá»•ng: 1_500_000, Withdraw: 100_000 â†’ cÃ²n: 1_400_000
        assertEquals(1_400_000.0, total, 0.001,
                "Tá»•ng balance + frozen pháº£i báº±ng tá»•ng Ä‘Ã£ náº¡p - Ä‘Ã£ rÃºt");
    }
}

package com.auction.domain;

import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

import java.time.LocalDateTime;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;

/**
 * Unit test cho {@link AuctionManager}.
 *
 * <p>CÃ¡c test nÃ y hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng khÃ´ng cáº§n Database â€” wallet vÃ  DAO
 * Ä‘Æ°á»£c xá»­ lÃ½ best-effort (báº¯t ngoáº¡i lá»‡ bÃªn trong AuctionManager).</p>
 */
@DisplayName("AuctionManager â€” Unit Tests")
class AuctionManagerTest {

    private AuctionManager manager;

    @BeforeEach
    void setUp() {
        manager = AuctionManager.getInstance();
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Táº¡o & Quáº£n lÃ½ phiÃªn
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Táº¡o phiÃªn má»›i, start, bid, vÃ  close â€” luá»“ng hoÃ n chá»‰nh")
    void fullFlow_createStartBidClose_shouldFollowExpectedStates() {
        String auctionId = "FLOW-" + System.nanoTime();

        // Táº¡o vÃ  start phiÃªn
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        assertTrue(manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-1", "SESSION-ITEM", "SELLER-1", 100.0, now.plusHours(1), now.plusHours(2)),
                "Táº¡o phiÃªn má»›i pháº£i thÃ nh cÃ´ng");
        assertTrue(manager.startSession(auctionId),
                "Start phiÃªn PENDING pháº£i thÃ nh cÃ´ng");

        // Äáº·t giÃ¡ (wallet khÃ´ng cÃ³ trong test â†’ bá» qua, bid váº«n Ä‘Æ°á»£c ghi nháº­n)
        boolean bidOk = manager.placeBid(auctionId, "BIDDER-1", 150.0);
        assertTrue(bidOk, "Bid há»£p lá»‡ pháº£i Ä‘Æ°á»£c cháº¥p nháº­n");

        // ÄÃ³ng phiÃªn
        assertTrue(manager.closeSession(auctionId), "Close phiÃªn RUNNING pháº£i thÃ nh cÃ´ng");

        // Kiá»ƒm tra tráº¡ng thÃ¡i cuá»‘i
        AuctionSession session = manager.getSession(auctionId);
        assertNotNull(session);
        assertEquals(150.0,                   session.getCurrentHighestBid(), "GiÃ¡ pháº£i lÃ  150.0");
        assertEquals("BIDDER-1",             session.getWinnerID(),          "Winner pháº£i lÃ  BIDDER-1");
        assertEquals(AuctionStatus.SUCCESS, session.getStatus(),            "Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i pháº£i SUCCESS");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i táº¡o phiÃªn vá»›i ID Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i")
    void createSession_shouldRejectDuplicateAuctionId() {
        String auctionId = "DUP-" + System.nanoTime();

        assertTrue(manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-A", "SELLER-A", 200.0));
        assertFalse(manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-B", "SELLER-B", 300.0),
                "KhÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c táº¡o phiÃªn vá»›i ID Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i táº¡o phiÃªn vá»›i ID null hoáº·c rá»—ng")
    void createSession_shouldRejectBlankAuctionId() {
        assertFalse(manager.createSession(null,  "ITEM-X", "SELLER-X", 100.0), "null ID pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
        assertFalse(manager.createSession("",    "ITEM-X", "SELLER-X", 100.0), "empty ID pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
        assertFalse(manager.createSession("   ", "ITEM-X", "SELLER-X", 100.0), "blank ID pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Äáº·t giÃ¡ qua AuctionManager
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid vÃ o phiÃªn khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i")
    void placeBid_shouldReturnFalseForUnknownAuction() {
        boolean result = manager.placeBid("NONEXISTENT-AUCTION", "BIDDER-X", 999.0);
        assertFalse(result, "Bid vÃ o phiÃªn khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid vÃ o phiÃªn chÆ°a RUNNING (tráº¡ng thÃ¡i OPEN)")
    void placeBid_shouldRejectWhenSessionNotRunning() {
        String auctionId = "NOTRUN-" + System.nanoTime();
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-NR", "ITEM-NR", "SELLER-NR", 100.0, now.plusHours(1), now.plusHours(2));
        // KhÃ´ng gá»i startSession â†’ tráº¡ng thÃ¡i váº«n lÃ  PENDING

        assertFalse(manager.placeBid(auctionId, "BIDDER-NR", 150.0),
                "Bid vÃ o phiÃªn PENDING pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Bid thá»© hai pháº£i tháº¯ng bid thá»© nháº¥t náº¿u giÃ¡ cao hÆ¡n")
    void placeBid_secondHigherBidShouldWin() {
        String auctionId = "BID2-" + System.nanoTime();
        manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-B2", "ITEM-B2", "SELLER-B2", 100.0, 60);
        manager.startSession(auctionId);

        manager.placeBid(auctionId, "BIDDER-A", 200.0);
        manager.placeBid(auctionId, "BIDDER-B", 350.0); // VÆ°á»£t máº·t

        AuctionSession session = manager.getSession(auctionId);
        assertEquals(350.0,     session.getCurrentHighestBid());
        assertEquals("BIDDER-B", session.getWinnerID());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid tháº¥p hÆ¡n giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i trong phiÃªn RUNNING")
    void placeBid_lowerBidShouldBeRejected() {
        String auctionId = "LOW-" + System.nanoTime();
        manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-LOW", "ITEM-LOW", "SELLER-LOW", 100.0, 60);
        manager.startSession(auctionId);

        manager.placeBid(auctionId, "BIDDER-X", 500.0); // Bid Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn

        boolean rejected = manager.placeBid(auctionId, "BIDDER-Y", 300.0); // Tháº¥p hÆ¡n

        assertFalse(rejected, "Bid tháº¥p hÆ¡n pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
        assertEquals("BIDDER-X", manager.getSession(auctionId).getWinnerID());
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Start / Close session
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    @Test
    @DisplayName("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ start phiÃªn Ä‘Ã£ RUNNING")
    void startSession_shouldRejectAlreadyRunningSession() {
        String auctionId = "START-RUN-" + System.nanoTime();
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-SR", "ITEM-SR", "SELLER-SR", 100.0, now.plusHours(1), now.plusHours(2));
        assertTrue(manager.startSession(auctionId), "Láº§n 1 start PENDING thÃ nh cÃ´ng");
        assertFalse(manager.startSession(auctionId), "KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ start phiÃªn Ä‘ang RUNNING");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ close phiÃªn khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i")
    void closeSession_shouldReturnFalseForUnknownSession() {
        assertFalse(manager.closeSession("GHOST-SESSION-XYZ"),
                "Close phiÃªn khÃ´ng tá»“n táº¡i pháº£i tráº£ false");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ close phiÃªn Ä‘Ã£ FINISHED")
    void closeSession_shouldRejectFinishedSession() {
        String auctionId = "DONE-" + System.nanoTime();
        manager.createSession(auctionId, "ITEM-DN", "SELLER-DN", 100.0);
        manager.startSession(auctionId);
        manager.closeSession(auctionId); // ÄÃ³ng láº§n 1

        assertFalse(manager.closeSession(auctionId), "Close phiÃªn Ä‘Ã£ FINISHED pháº£i tráº£ false");
    }
}

package com.auction.domain;

import com.auction.common.dto.BidResult;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.DisplayName;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

import java.time.LocalDateTime;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;

/**
 * Unit test cho {@link AuctionSession}.
 *
 * <p><strong>KhÃ´ng phá»¥ thuá»™c Database</strong> â€” sau khi refactor,
 * AuctionSession lÃ  pure domain object khÃ´ng cÃ³ I/O.</p>
 */
@DisplayName("AuctionSession â€” Unit Tests")
class AuctionSessionTest {

    private static final String AUCTION_ID = "TEST-001";
    private static final String ITEM_ID    = "ITEM-001";
    private static final String ITEM_NAME  = "Laptop Test";
    private static final String SELLER_ID  = "SELLER-001";
    private static final double START_PRICE = 1_000_000.0;

    private AuctionSession session;

    @BeforeEach
    void setUp() {
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        session = new AuctionSession(
                AUCTION_ID, ITEM_ID, ITEM_NAME, SELLER_ID,
                START_PRICE, now, now.plusHours(1));
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Tá»« chá»‘i bid khi phiÃªn chÆ°a RUNNING
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid khi phiÃªn chÆ°a Ä‘Æ°á»£c báº¯t Ä‘áº§u (PENDING)")
    void processBid_shouldRejectWhenStatusIsPending() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.PENDING);
        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0);

        assertFalse(result.success, "PhiÃªn PENDING khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c nháº­n bid");
        assertEquals(START_PRICE, session.getCurrentHighestBid(), "GiÃ¡ khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c thay Ä‘á»•i");
        assertNull(session.getWinnerID(), "KhÃ´ng cÃ³ winner");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Cháº¥p nháº­n bid há»£p lá»‡
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("Cháº¥p nháº­n bid há»£p lá»‡ vÃ  cáº­p nháº­t giÃ¡ + winner")
    void processBid_shouldAcceptValidBidAndUpdateState() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);
        double bidAmount = 1_500_000.0;

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-1", bidAmount);

        assertTrue(result.success, "Bid há»£p lá»‡ pháº£i Ä‘Æ°á»£c cháº¥p nháº­n");
        assertEquals(bidAmount, session.getCurrentHighestBid(), "GiÃ¡ pháº£i Ä‘Æ°á»£c cáº­p nháº­t");
        assertEquals("BIDDER-1", session.getWinnerID(), "Winner pháº£i lÃ  ngÆ°á»i vá»«a bid");
        assertNotNull(result.transaction, "Pháº£i cÃ³ BidTransaction");
        assertEquals("BIDDER-1", result.transaction.getBidderID());
        assertEquals(bidAmount, result.transaction.getBidAmount());
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Tá»« chá»‘i bid tháº¥p hÆ¡n hoáº·c báº±ng giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid tháº¥p hÆ¡n giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i")
    void processBid_shouldRejectBidLowerThanCurrentPrice() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);
        session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0); // Bid Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-2", 1_500_000.0); // Tháº¥p hÆ¡n

        assertFalse(result.success, "Bid tháº¥p hÆ¡n pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
        assertEquals(2_000_000.0, session.getCurrentHighestBid(), "GiÃ¡ khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c thay Ä‘á»•i");
        assertEquals("BIDDER-1", session.getWinnerID(), "Winner khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c thay Ä‘á»•i");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid báº±ng Ä‘Ãºng giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i")
    void processBid_shouldRejectBidEqualToCurrentPrice() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-1", START_PRICE);

        assertFalse(result.success, "Bid báº±ng giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i pháº£i bá»‹ tá»« chá»‘i");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // ThÃ´ng tin hoÃ n tiá»n (refund) cho ngÆ°á»i dáº«n Ä‘áº§u cÅ©
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("Cung cáº¥p thÃ´ng tin hoÃ n tiá»n cho bidder cÅ© khi cÃ³ bid má»›i")
    void processBid_shouldReturnRefundInfoForPreviousLeader() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);
        session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0); // Bid Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-2", 3_000_000.0); // VÆ°á»£t máº·t

        assertTrue(result.success);
        assertEquals("BIDDER-1", result.refundBidderID, "Pháº£i hoÃ n tiá»n cho BIDDER-1");
        assertEquals(2_000_000.0, result.refundAmount, "Sá»‘ tiá»n hoÃ n pháº£i Ä‘Ãºng");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("Bid Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn khÃ´ng cÃ³ refundBidderID (chÆ°a cÃ³ ngÆ°á»i dáº«n Ä‘áº§u cÅ©)")
    void processBid_firstBidShouldHaveNullRefund() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0);

        assertTrue(result.success);
        assertNull(result.refundBidderID, "Bid Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn khÃ´ng cáº§n hoÃ n tiá»n cho ai");
        assertEquals(0.0, result.refundAmount);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Anti-sniping (gia háº¡n tá»± Ä‘á»™ng)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("Anti-sniping: gia háº¡n phiÃªn khi cÃ³ bid trong 30 giÃ¢y cuá»‘i")
    void processBid_shouldExtendTimeWhenBidInLastThirtySeconds() {
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        session = new AuctionSession(AUCTION_ID, ITEM_ID, ITEM_NAME, SELLER_ID,
                START_PRICE, now, now.plusSeconds(20)); // CÃ²n 20 giÃ¢y
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);
        LocalDateTime originalEnd = session.getEndTime();

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0);

        assertTrue(result.success);
        assertEquals(AuctionStatus.EXTENDED, session.getStatus(), "Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i pháº£i lÃ  EXTENDED");
        assertTrue(session.getEndTime().isAfter(originalEnd.plusSeconds(59)),
                "Thá»i gian pháº£i Ä‘Æ°á»£c gia háº¡n thÃªm 60 giÃ¢y");
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("KhÃ´ng gia háº¡n náº¿u bid xuáº¥t hiá»‡n khi cÃ²n nhiá»u thá»i gian")
    void processBid_shouldNotExtendTimeWhenPlentyOfTimeLeft() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING); // CÃ²n 1 giá»
        LocalDateTime originalEnd = session.getEndTime();

        session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0);

        assertEquals(AuctionStatus.RUNNING, session.getStatus(), "Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i khÃ´ng Ä‘á»•i");
        assertEquals(originalEnd, session.getEndTime(), "Thá»i gian káº¿t thÃºc khÃ´ng Ä‘á»•i");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // PhiÃªn háº¿t giá»
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("Tá»« chá»‘i bid sau khi phiÃªn háº¿t giá» vÃ  chuyá»ƒn sang FAILED")
    void processBid_shouldRejectAndFinishWhenTimeExpired() {
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        session = new AuctionSession(AUCTION_ID, ITEM_ID, ITEM_NAME, SELLER_ID,
                START_PRICE, now.minusHours(2), now.minusSeconds(1)); // ÄÃ£ háº¿t giá»
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);

        BidResult result = session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0);

        assertFalse(result.success, "PhiÃªn háº¿t giá» khÃ´ng Ä‘Æ°á»£c nháº­n bid");
        assertEquals(AuctionStatus.FAILED, session.getStatus(), "Tráº¡ng thÃ¡i pháº£i lÃ  FAILED");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Lá»‹ch sá»­ giao dá»‹ch
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    @Test
    @DisplayName("BidHistory lÆ°u Ä‘Ãºng sá»‘ giao dá»‹ch thÃ nh cÃ´ng")
    void processBid_shouldRecordAllSuccessfulBids() {
        session.setStatus(AuctionStatus.RUNNING);

        session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 2_000_000.0);
        session.processBid("BIDDER-2", 3_000_000.0);
        session.processBid("BIDDER-1", 4_000_000.0);
        session.processBid("BIDDER-2", 2_500_000.0); // Tháº¥t báº¡i â€” tháº¥p hÆ¡n giÃ¡ hiá»‡n táº¡i

        assertEquals(3, session.getBidHistory().size(), "Pháº£i cÃ³ Ä‘Ãºng 3 bid thÃ nh cÃ´ng");
        assertEquals(4_000_000.0, session.getCurrentHighestBid());
        assertEquals("BIDDER-1", session.getWinnerID());
    }
}
